through multiple layers of validation and sanitization mechanisms:\\n\\n## Header Validation Framework\\n\\nThe primary header validation implementation is located in `source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/`. This directory contains the core header validation logic for HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, and HTTP/3:\\n\\n**Header Validator Core (header_validator.cc/h):**\\n- Implements abstract `HeaderValidator` base class with protocol-agnostic validation methods\\n- `validateGenericHeaderName()` validates header names against RFC 9110 token definition using character tables to reject invalid characters that could enable injection attacks\\n- `validateGenericHeaderValue()` validates header values by checking each character against `kGenericHeaderValueCharTable` to prevent control characters (including CR/LF needed for CRLF injection)\\n- `validatePathHeaderCharacters()` validates URI paths to prevent injection\\n- `validateContentLengthHeader()` validates Content-Length values as numeric integers\\n- `validateHostHeader()` validates Host/Authority headers including detection of deprecated userinfo component (@ character)\\n- `validateMethodHeader()` validates HTTP method names\\n- `validateSchemeHeader()` validates scheme pseudo-headers (http/https)\\n- `sanitizeHeadersWithUnderscores()` drops or rejects headers with underscores based on configuration\\n\\n**HTTP/1 Validation (http1_header_validator.cc/h):**\\n- `ServerHttp1HeaderValidator` and `ClientHttp1HeaderValidator` implement protocol-specific validation\\n- `validateRequestHeaders()` validates entire HTTP/1 request header map including Transfer-Encoding and Content-Length\\n- `sanitizeContentLength()` handles Content-Length and Transfer-Encoding validation per RFC 9112\\n\\n**HTTP/2 Validation (http2_header_validator.cc/h):**\\n- `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator` and `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator` implement HTTP/2-specific validation\\n- Validates pseudo-headers (`:method`, `:path`, `:scheme`, `:authority`)\\n- Additional character set validation for path headers that differs from HTTP/1\\n\\n## Character Validation Tables\\n\\n**Character Tables (character_tables.h):**\\n- `kGenericHeaderValueCharTable`: Allows visible ASCII characters (0x21-0x7E) and extended ASCII (0x80-0xFF), crucially excluding CR (0x0D), LF (0x0A), and NULL (0x00) to prevent CRLF injection\\n- `kGenericHeaderNameCharTable`: RFC 9110 token characters (alphanumeric and special chars) for header names\\n- `kPathHeaderCharTable`: RFC 3986 compliant characters for URL paths\\n- `kMethodHeaderCharTable`: RFC 9110 tchar set for HTTP methods\\n\\n**Character Set Validation (character_set_validation.h):**\\n- `testCharInTable()` utility function uses bit-packed character tables for efficient O(1) character validation\\n\\n## Internal Header Stripping (Forbidden Headers)\\n\\n**Connection Manager Utility (conn_manager_utility.cc):**\\n- `cleanInternalHeaders()` function removes internal/private headers to prevent downstream exposure and injection:\\n  - Edge request headers stripped: `x-envoy-decorator-operation`, `x-envoy-downstream-service-cluster`, `x-envoy-downstream-service-node`, `x-envoy-original-path`\\n  - All request headers stripped: `x-envoy-retriable-status-codes`, `x-envoy-retriable-header-names`, `x-envoy-retry-on`, `x-envoy-retry-grpc-on`, `x-envoy-max-retries`, `x-envoy-upstream-alt-stat-name`, `x-envoy-upstream-request-timeout-ms`, `x-envoy-upstream-request-per-try-timeout-ms`, `x-envoy-upstream-request-timeout-alt-response`, `x-envoy-expected-request-timeout-ms`, `x-envoy-force-trace`, `x-envoy-ip-tags`, `x-envoy-original-url`, `x-envoy-hedge-on-per-try-timeout`\\n  - Configurable internal-only headers removed via `request_headers.remove(header)` calls\\n\\n## Header Utility Functions\\n\\n**Header Utility (header_utility.cc/h):**\\n- `headerNameIsValid()`: Validates header names per RFC 7230\\n- `headerValueIsValid()`: Validates header values per RFC 7230\\n- `headerNameContainsUnderscore()`: Detects headers with underscores for optional rejection\\n- `stripTrailingHostDot()`: Removes trailing dots from host headers\\n- `stripPortFromHost()`: Removes or validates port in host header\\n- `isEnvoyInternalRequest()`: Detects internal Envoy requests\\n\\n## Path Normalization and Sanitization\\n\\n**Path Normalizer (path_normalizer.cc/h):**\\n- `sanitizePathWithFragment()`: Strips fragments from URL paths to prevent injection\\n- `sanitizeEncodedSlashes()`: Handles percent-encoded slash characters per configuration\\n- Supports path normalization with configurable behavior for non-compliant characters\\n\\n## HTTP Codec Implementations\\n\\n**HTTP/1 Codec (http1/codec_impl.cc):**\\n- Handles raw HTTP/1 header parsing with CRLF sequence detection\\n- Validates headers during parsing phase before they enter the validation framework\\n\\n**HTTP/2 Codec (http2/codec_impl.cc):**\\n- HTTP/2 uses binary framing, inherently preventing CRLF injection\\n- Headers validated by header validator framework after decoding from binary format\\n\\n## Validation Chain\\n\\nThe validation flow for incoming HTTP/1 requests:\\n1. `conn_manager_impl.cc`: Connection manager receives request\\n2. HTTP codec parses raw bytes (http1/codec_impl.cc)\\n3. `http1_header_validator.cc::validateRequestHeaders()` performs validation\\n4. Character validation via `header_validator.cc::validateGenericHeaderName/Value()` using character tables\\n5. `source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/`. This directory contains the core header validation logic for HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, and HTTP/3:\\n\\n**Header Validator Core (header_validator.cc/h):**\\n- Implements abstract `HeaderValidator` base class with protocol-agnostic validation methods\\n- `validateGenericHeaderName()` validates header names against RFC 9110 token definition using character tables to reject invalid characters that could enable injection attacks\\n- `validateGenericHeaderValue()` validates header values by checking each character against `kGenericHeaderValueCharTable` to prevent control characters (including CR/LF needed for CRLF injection)\\n- `validatePathHeaderCharacters()` validates URI paths to prevent injection\\n- `validateContentLengthHeader()` validates Content-Length values as numeric integers\\n- `validateHostHeader()` validates Host/Authority headers including detection of deprecated userinfo component (@ character)\\n- `validateMethodHeader()` validates HTTP method names\\n- `validateSchemeHeader()` validates scheme pseudo-headers (http/https)\\n- `sanitizeHeadersWithUnderscores()` drops or rejects headers with underscores based on configuration\\n\\n**HTTP/1 Validation (http1_header_validator.cc/h):**\\n- `ServerHttp1HeaderValidator` and `ClientHttp1HeaderValidator` implement protocol-specific validation\\n- `validateRequestHeaders()` validates entire HTTP/1 request header map including Transfer-Encoding and Content-Length\\n- `sanitizeContentLength()` handles Content-Length and Transfer-Encoding validation per RFC 9112\\n\\n**HTTP/2 Validation (http2_header_validator.cc/h):**\\n- `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator` and `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator` implement HTTP/2-specific validation\\n- Validates pseudo-headers (`:method`, `:path`, `:scheme`, `:authority`)\\n- Additional character set validation for path headers that differs from HTTP/1\\n\\n## Character Validation Tables\\n\\n**Character Tables (character_tables.h):**\\n- `kGenericHeaderValueCharTable`: Allows visible ASCII characters (0x21-0x7E) and extended ASCII (0x80-0xFF), crucially excluding CR (0x0D), LF (0x0A), and NULL (0x00) to prevent CRLF injection\\n- `kGenericHeaderNameCharTable`: RFC 9110 token characters (alphanumeric and special chars) for header names\\n- `kPathHeaderCharTable`: RFC 3986 compliant characters for URL paths\\n- `kMethodHeaderCharTable`: RFC 9110 tchar set for HTTP methods\\n\\n**Character Set Validation (character_set_validation.h):**\\n- `testCharInTable()` utility function uses bit-packed character tables for efficient O(1) character validation\\n\\n## Internal Header Stripping (Forbidden Headers)\\n\\n**Connection Manager Utility (conn_manager_utility.cc):**\\n- `cleanInternalHeaders()` function removes internal/private headers to prevent downstream exposure and injection:\\n  - Edge request headers stripped: `x-envoy-decorator-operation`, `x-envoy-downstream-service-cluster`, `x-envoy-downstream-service-node`, `x-envoy-original-path`\\n  - All request headers stripped: `x-envoy-retriable-status-codes`, `x-envoy-retriable-header-names`, `x-envoy-retry-on`, requests\\n\\n## Path Normalization and Sanitization\\n\\n**Path Normalizer (path_normalizer.cc/h):**\\n- `sanitizePathWithFragment()`: Strips fragments from URL paths to prevent injection\\n- `sanitizeEncodedSlashes()`: Handles percent-encoded slash characters per configuration\\n- Supports path normalization with configurable behavior for non-compliant characters\\n\\n## HTTP Codec Implementations\\n\\n**HTTP/1 Codec (http1/codec_impl.cc):**\\n- Handles raw HTTP/1 header parsing with CRLF sequence detection\\n- Validates headers during parsing phase before they enter the validation framework\\n\\n**HTTP/2 Codec (http2/codec_impl.cc):**\\n- HTTP/2 uses binary framing, inherently preventing CRLF injection\\n- Headers validated by header validator framework after decoding from binary format\\n\\n## Validation Chain\\n\\nThe validation flow for incoming HTTP/1 requests:\\n1. `conn_manager_impl.cc`: Connection manager receives request\\n2. HTTP codec parses raw bytes (http1/codec_impl.cc)\\n3. `http1_header_validator.cc::validateRequestHeaders()` performs validation\\n4.
